Glazed only in the inside, the final earth tones and textures are the result of the different combination of clays exposed to the heat of the kiln fire. Weight: 0.5 lbs Please note: This type of ceramic has different percentages of earths and clays in order to "pigment" the paste without the need to apply a colored glaze. The materials reacts directly to contact with fire, the heat influences the intensity of color that each piece can have and sometimes there are variations even in the same batch, which is why in a single finish there can be a wide range of tones.

The weaving is a traditional technique that has been passed along from one generation to the next. Women gather to weave and connect with each other under the shade of large trees with their children playing nearby. Each weaver infuses her own touch in these baskets, so each one is unique in pattern and shape - no two are identical, which makes each basket truly one of a kind. Use these gorgeous baskets to decorate any space that needs a warm, handmade touch. Amazing on their own or with dried flowers, stems or branches. They look best in groups of different sizes for a fuller effect. The baskets are measured using a soft tape measure. The tape is run from the center of the base of the basket, around the curve of the bowl, then up the neck. Because of the wide variety of shapes of these baskets, the measurement is a CONTOUR measurement, not a straight LxWxH. You need to choose mainland China, then find this device, and then connect, because the amplifier is in Chiness version What do the different colors of the indicator light mean? The blue light is always on: the amplifier is running normally, and the WiFi pairing is successful. The yellow light is always on: the amplifier is starting up, the process is very short, about 10 seconds. Blinking blue: Waiting for pairing, pairing, or pairing failed.The pairing failed. The original network's WiFi  may be changed or it may be far from the original network. Steady red light: The boot failed, please re-plug and try to repair. If the problem persists, please call after-sales service. Why The amplifier is always flashing orange, then the blue light is flashing? The initial setting was unsuccessful. After inserting the Xiaomi router USB, the pairing could not be completed. Please upgrade your router to the latest development or stable version (2.0 or above) Check if the amplifier has been paired. If it has been paired, please reset the amplifier to the factory settings (hold the reset hole with the card pin for 5 seconds), then re-pair The paired amplifier appears blue flashing Try plugging or unplugging the amplifier, or reset the amplifier (use the PIN pin to hold the reset hole for 5 seconds) before re-pairing How to customize the network name and  of the amplifier? - [Recycled Bomb Chopsticks](https://beatbargains-2.myshopify.com/products/recycled-bomb-chopsticks): Turning war into peace, t hese recycled bombshell chopsticks carry a meaningful message and give back to a community once devastated by bombing. These truly unique chopsticks will be the conversation piece of any meal! Material: Recycled aluminum bomb parts Measurements: L 8.25" Handmade with love in Laos As with all handcrafted goods, there are slight variations making each piece a work of art and truly one of a kind. Care: Hand wash Artisan Profile Laos is the most heavily bombed country per capita in the world. From 1963-1973, Laos became an unwitting pawn during the Second Indochinese War. During this time, the US Air Force dropped a planeload of cluster bombs every eight minutes for nine consecutive years. Right after the war, villagers began gathering aluminum from exploded bombs and made it into spoons. The villagers were taught this skill by a family that relocated to Ban Naphia from Houaphan Province, further north. In the early days, five families produced the recycled bomb spoons. Today, there are approximately 13 families producing more than 150,000 spoons per year from war and non-war scrap aluminum. Production has expanded to include bracelets, earrings, and pendants. We work with artisans in Ban Naphia located in the Xieng Khuang Province who source aluminum from airplane parts and bombs dropped throughout Laos during the Secret War (Vietnam War) in the 1960s. The community which produces the recycled bomb products have all been trained by Helvetas, a Swiss NGO, on how to handle the metals safely, including smelting and cleaning the aluminum before use. It is important to note that of all the bombs dropped in Laos, 30% did not explode. Unexploded ordnance (UXO) continues to pose a significant threat to the safety of villagers in rural Lao. In their search for scrap metal, many villagers encounter UXO and suffer catastrophic injuries. The generous spirit and ingenuity of Lao artisans is evident in our collection of recycled bomb products. War and persistent air raids in the 1960s left the countryside littered with bomb and metal shrapnel. The remnants of this legacy have been transformed into emblems of peace.

These are totally natural and very nutritious dog chews made from yak's milk and cow's milk and free from artificial ingredients. Tje milk is processed to remove lactose and make the chews easily digestible and very gentle for sensitive stomachs. No Odor, No Stains This is a highly nutritious product for dogs that can provide many hours of chew time for your dog. Long-Lasting for Aggressive Chewers Our Gold dog chew treats are 6 inch to 8 inches long and harder than other treats which give them a longer chewing lifespan - perfect for puppies and dogs that love to gnaw. Microwavable for a Softer Chew Does your dog prefer a softer treat or have baby teeth, cracked teeth or broken teeth? - [Women’s Health Multivitamins](https://beatbargains-2.myshopify.com/products/women-s-health-multivitamins): My Balance Women’s Multivitamin My Balance Women’s Multivitamins offer a robust blend of essential vitamins and minerals tailored to support various aspects of overall well-being. Each serving is meticulously formulated to provide a broad spectrum of nutrients, ensuring that women receive balanced nutritional support. Key Ingredients and Their Roles 1. Biotin: Biotin, also known as Vitamin B7, is a water-soluble B vitamin found in various foods. It plays a role in converting food into energy and is often associated with supporting healthy skin, hair, and nails. 2. Vitamin A: This fat-soluble vitamin is crucial for maintaining normal vision, supporting immune function, and promoting cell growth. It is commonly found in foods such as carrots and sweet potatoes. 3. Vitamin C: As a water-soluble vitamin, Vitamin C is well-known for its role in the formation of collagen, a protein necessary for skin and connective tissues. It is also found in fruits like oranges and strawberries. 4. Calcium: Essential for bone health, calcium is a key mineral that helps maintain strong bones and teeth. It is commonly obtained from dairy products and leafy green vegetables. 5. Iron: Iron is a crucial mineral involved in the production of hemoglobin, which helps transport oxygen in the blood. It is found in foods like red meat, legumes, and fortified cereals. 6. Vitamin D3: Vitamin D3, a form of Vitamin D, is vital for calcium absorption and bone health. It is synthesized by the body when exposed to sunlight and is also found in fatty fish. 7. Vitamin E: This fat-soluble antioxidant helps protect cells from damage and is found in nuts, seeds, and vegetable oils. 8. Vitamin B1 (Thiamine): Thiamine is involved in carbohydrate metabolism and supports nerve function. It is found in whole grains, pork, and legumes. 9. Vitamin B6 (Pyridoxine): Vitamin B6 plays a role in amino acid metabolism and neurotransmitter synthesis. It is found in poultry, fish, and bananas. 10. Folate (Vitamin B9): Folate is essential for DNA synthesis and cell division. It is found in leafy green vegetables, legumes, and fortified foods. 11. Vitamin B12 (Cobalamin): Vitamin B12 is important for red blood cell formation and neurological function. It is found in animal products such as meat, dairy, and eggs. 12. Vitamin B5 (Pantothenic Acid): Vitamin B5 supports energy metabolism and the synthesis of coenzyme A. It is present in foods like eggs, avocados, and whole grains. 13. Magnesium: Magnesium is involved in over 300 biochemical reactions in the body, including energy production and muscle function. It is found in nuts, seeds, and leafy greens. 14. Zinc: Zinc supports immune function and is involved in numerous enzymatic processes. It is found in meat, shellfish, and legumes. 15. Manganese: Manganese is a trace mineral that plays a role in bone formation and metabolism. It is found in whole grains, nuts, and leafy vegetables. 16. Potassium: Potassium helps regulate fluid balance, muscle contractions, and nerve signals. It is abundant in fruits, vegetables, and legumes. 17. Proprietary Blend: This unique blend includes: - Horsetail Extract: Derived from the horsetail plant, this ingredient is often included for its traditional use in supporting hair, skin, and nail health. - Nettle Root: Nettle root has been traditionally used to support general health and wellness. - Spirulina: A type of blue-green algae rich in protein and various nutrients, often used for its nutritional profile. - Saw Palmetto: Extracted from the berries of the saw palmetto plant, this ingredient is included for its traditional uses. Product Details - Form: Available in easy-to-swallow capsules. - Quantity: Each bottle contains 60 capsules. My Balance Women’s Multivitamins are designed to provide a comprehensive range of essential nutrients that support daily wellness. This formula is crafted to complement a balanced diet and lifestyle.
